<script>

    function saveSession(sport) 
    {
        $.ajax({
			url: 'sess.php',
			type: "POST",
			data: {sport_s: sport},
			success: function() {
				window.location.reload(true);
			}
		});
		
    }

</script>

<script>
$(function() {
	$('body').addClass('collapsed');
	$('.nav-toggle').on('click', function() {
		if ($('#main-navigation').hasClass('expanded')) {
			$('#main-navigation').toggleClass('expanded');
			$('body').toggleClass('expanded');
			document.cookie = "leftBar=collapsed; path=/; expires=Fri, 31 Dec 9999 23:59:59 GMT";
		} else {
			$('#main-navigation').toggleClass('expanded');
			$('body').toggleClass('expanded');
			document.cookie = "leftBar=expanded; path=/; expires=Fri, 31 Dec 9999 23:59:59 GMT";
		}
	});
	$('.nav-comp-toggle').on('click', function() {
		$('.nav-sports').hide();
		$('.nav-comps').animate({width: 'toggle'});
	});
	$('.nav-sport-toggle').on('click', function() {
		$('.nav-comps').hide();
		$('.nav-sports').animate({width: 'toggle'});
	});
	$('.nav-sport').on('click', function() {
		var sport = $(this).data('id');
		$.ajax({
			url: 'sess.php',
			type: "POST",
			data: {sport_s: sport},
			success: function() {
				window.location.reload(true);
			}
		});
	});
	
	$('.nav-search input').on('input', function() {
		var val = $(this).val().toLowerCase();
		var items = $(this).parent().parent().find('.nav-item-wrapper > *');
		
		if (val != '') {
			items.hide();
			
			items.each(function(el) {
				if ($(this).text().toLowerCase().indexOf(val) >= 0) {
					$(this).show();
				}
			});
		} else {
			items.show();
		}
	});
});

</script>

<link rel="stylesheet" href="https://ajax.googleapis.com/ajax/libs/jqueryui/1.10.1/themes/base/minified/jquery-ui.min.css" type="text/css" />
<link rel="stylesheet" href="//cdnjs.cloudflare.com/ajax/libs/select2/4.0.1/css/select2.min.css">
<script type="text/javascript" src="https://code.jquery.com/ui/1.10.1/jquery-ui.min.js"></script>
<script src="//cdnjs.cloudflare.com/ajax/libs/select2/4.0.1/js/select2.min.js"></script>
<script type="text/javascript">    
$(function() {
	$('select.matchtoday_row').on('change', function() {
		$(this).closest('.resutrow').find('.change-check').prop('checked', true);
	}); 
	$(".limitedNumbChosen").select2({
		placeholder: "Select Broadcaster(s)"
	});
	$(".limitedNumbChosen").on('select2:selecting', function(e) {
		$(this).closest('.match-row').find('.change-check').prop('checked', true);
	});
	$(".auto").autocomplete({
		source: "./internal/autosearch_venues.php?sport=soccer",
		minLength: 2
	});	
	$(".auto-referee").autocomplete({
		source: "./internal/autosearch_referees.php?sport=soccer",
		minLength: 2
	});
	$(".auto-captain").autocomplete({
		source: function(request, response) {
			var el = this.element;
			var ph = el.prop('placeholder');
			ph = ph.split(' ');
			var team = ph[1];
			var mid = el.parent().parent().find('span').first().find('a').eq(1).text();
			$.ajax({
				url: './internal/mt2_captain.php',
				type: 'POST',
				dataType: 'json',
				data: {term: request.term,mid:mid,team:team},
				success: function (data) {
					response(data);
				}
			});
        },	
		minLength: 2
	});
	$(".auto-coach").autocomplete({
		source: function(request, response) {
			var el = this.element;
			var ph = el.prop('placeholder');
			ph = ph.split(' ');
			var team = ph[1];
			//var mid = el.parent().parent().find('span').first().find('a').eq(1).text();
			var mid = el.closest('.match-row').data('id');
			$.ajax({
				url: './internal/mt2_coach.php',
				type: 'POST',
				dataType: 'json',
				data: {term: request.term,mid:mid,team:team},
				success: function (data) {
					response(data);
				}
			});
        },	
		minLength: 2
	});
	$(".auto-coach2").autocomplete({
		source: function(request, response) {
			var el = this.element;
			var team = $('#coach-team').val();
			$.ajax({
				url: './internal/mt2_coach.php',
				type: 'POST',
				dataType: 'json',
				data: {term: request.term,season_id:77207,team:team},
				success: function (data) {
					response(data);
				}
			});
        },	
		minLength: 2
	});
	
	
	$('body').on('click', '.curling-hammer', function() {
		if ($(this).hasClass('active')) {
			$(this).removeClass('active');
			$(this).parent().parent().find('.curling-hammer-team').val('');   
		} else {
			$(this).parent().parent().find('.curling-hammer').removeClass('active');
			$(this).addClass('active');
			$(this).parent().parent().find('.curling-hammer-team').val($(this).data('id')); 
		}
		$(this).closest('.match-row').find('.change-check').prop('checked', true);
	});
	
	
	$('body').on('click', '.contestant-type-change', function() {
		if ($(this).parent().find('.sub-contestant').css('display') == 'block') {
			$(this).parent().find('.sub-contestant').hide();
			$(this).parent().find('.sub-contestant-team').show();
		} else {
			$(this).parent().find('.sub-contestant').show();
			$(this).parent().find('.sub-contestant-team').hide();
		}
	});
	$('.sub-match-toggle').on('click', function() {
		var matchId = $(this).parent().data('id');
		var container = $(this).parent().next('.sub-match-container');
		if (container.css('display') == 'block') {
			container.hide();
			container.empty();
			$(this).prop('src', 'https://dsg-backend.com/resources/img/icons/svg/plus-square.svg')
		} else {
			container.load("./internal/include/match_today/sub_matches.php?id=" + matchId + "&type=time");
			container.show();
			$(this).prop('src', 'https://dsg-backend.com/resources/img/icons/svg/minus-square.svg')
		}
		
	});
	$('#coach-team-add').on('click', function() {
		var team = $('#coach-team').val();
		var val = $(".auto-coach2").val();
		if (team != '' && val != '') {
			$('.coach-team-'+team).val(val);
			$('.coach-team-'+team+'-cb').prop('checked', true);;
		}
	});
	$('.select-status').on('change', function() {
		if ($(this).val() == 'Tech Knockout' || $(this).val() == 'Knockout' || $(this).val() == 'Awarded' || $(this).val() == 'Retired' || $(this).val() == 'Bye') {
			$(this).closest('.match-row').find('.select-winner').show();
		} else {
			$(this).closest('.match-row').find('.select-winner').hide();
		}
	});
});
</script>
